
vbs to generate model data -- followed by the output
--------------------------------------------------

function m
dim cs,c,n
set cs = cp.csNew()
if ( cs.open( "content" )) then
  do
    n = replace( cs.getText( "name" ), " ", "")
	if ( right( n,1 ) = "s" ) then
		n = left( n, len( n )-1)
	end if
	n = n & "Model"
    c = c & vbcrlf & vbcrlf & "---------------------------------------------"
    c = c & vbcrlf & n
    c = c & vbcrlf & getModelFields( cs.getInteger( "id" ))
    cs.goNext()
  loop while cs.ok
end if
cs.close()
call cp.file.saveVirtual( "Models.txt", c )
m = "<a href=""" & cp.site.filePath & "Models.txt"">Models.txt</a>"
end function

function getModelFields( contentId )
dim cs, t, p, l, s,d, fieldName
set cs = cp.csNew()
if ( cs.open( "content fields", "contentid=" & contentid, "name" )) then
  do
    fieldName = cs.getText( "name" )
	select case lcase( fieldName )
		case "id"
			p = p & ""
			l = vbcrlf & "." & fieldName & " = cs.getInteger(""" & fieldName & """)" & l
			s = s & ""
			d = d & ""
		case "contentcontrolid","modifiedby","createdby","createkey"
			p = p & ""
			l = l & vbcrlf & "." & fieldName & " = cs.getInteger(""" & fieldName & """)"
			s = s & vbcrlf & "cs.setField(""" & fieldName & """, " & fieldName & ".ToString())"
			d = d & vbcrlf & "instance." & fieldName & " = cdef.id"
		case "modifieddate","dateadded"
			p = p & ""
			l = l & vbcrlf & "." & fieldName & " = cs.getDate(""" & fieldName & """)"
			s = s & vbcrlf & "cs.setField(""" & fieldName & """, " & fieldName & ".ToString())"
			d = d & vbcrlf & "instance." & fieldName & " = genericController.EncodeDate(.fields(""" & fieldName & """).defaultValue)"
		case "name","sortorder","ccguid"
			p = p & ""
			l = l & vbcrlf & "." & fieldName & " = cs.getText(""" & fieldName & """)"
			s = s & vbcrlf & "cs.setField(""" & fieldName & """, " & fieldName & ")"
			d = d & vbcrlf & "instance." & fieldName & " = genericController.EncodeText(.fields(""" & fieldName & """).defaultValue)"
		case "active"
			p = p & ""
			l = l & vbcrlf & "." & fieldName & " = cs.getBoolean(""" & fieldName & """)"
			s = s & vbcrlf & "cs.setField(""" & fieldName & """, " & fieldName & ".ToString())"
			d = d & vbcrlf & "instance." & fieldName & " = genericController.EncodeBoolean(.fields(""" & fieldName & """).defaultValue)"
		case else
			select case cs.getInteger( "type" )
			  case 13: 
				' autoincrement (identity)
				p = p & vbcrlf & "public property " & fieldName & " as Integer"
				l = l & vbcrlf & "." & fieldName & " = cs.getInteger(""" & fieldName & """)"
				s = s & ""
				d = d & ""
			  case 1,7,15: 
				p = p & vbcrlf & "public property " & fieldName & " as Integer"
				l = l & vbcrlf & "." & fieldName & " = cs.getInteger(""" & fieldName & """)"
				s = s & vbcrlf & "cs.setField(""" & fieldName & """, " & fieldName & ".ToString())"
				d = d & vbcrlf & "instance." & fieldName & " = genericController.EncodeInteger(.fields(""" & fieldName & """).defaultValue)"
			  case 4:
				p = p & vbcrlf & "public property " & fieldName & " as Boolean"
				l = l & vbcrlf & "." & fieldName & " = cs.getBoolean(""" & fieldName & """)"
				s = s & vbcrlf & "cs.setField(""" & fieldName & """, " & fieldName & ".ToString())"
				d = d & vbcrlf & "instance." & fieldName & " = genericController.EncodeBoolean(.fields(""" & fieldName & """).defaultValue)"
			  case 2,3,6,10,11,16,17,18,19,20,21,22:
				p = p & vbcrlf & "public property " & fieldName & " as String"
				l = l & vbcrlf & "." & fieldName & " = cs.getText(""" & fieldName & """)"
				s = s & vbcrlf & "cs.setField(""" & fieldName & """, " & fieldName & ")"
				d = d & vbcrlf & "instance." & fieldName & " = genericController.EncodeText(.fields(""" & fieldName & """).defaultValue)"
			  case 5:
				p = p & vbcrlf & "public property " & fieldName & " as Date"
				l = l & vbcrlf & "." & fieldName & " = cs.getDate(""" & fieldName & """)"
				s = s & vbcrlf & "cs.setField(""" & fieldName & """, " & fieldName & ".ToString())"
				d = d & vbcrlf & "instance." & fieldName & " = genericController.EncodeDate(.fields(""" & fieldName & """).defaultValue)"
			  case 8,14:
				' ignore
			  case 9,12:
				p = p & vbcrlf & "public property " & fieldName & " as Double"
				l = l & vbcrlf & "." & fieldName & " = cs.getNumber(""" & fieldName & """)"
				s = s & vbcrlf & "cs.setField(""" & fieldName & """, " & fieldName & ".ToString())"
				d = d & vbcrlf & "instance." & fieldName & " = genericController.EncodeNumber(.fields(""" & fieldName & """).defaultValue)"
			end select
	end select
    cs.goNext()
  loop while cs.ok
  s = s & vbcrlf & "if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(ccGuid)) Then ccGuid = Controllers.genericController.getGUID()"
end if
cs.close()
getModelFields = p & vbcrlf & l & vbcrlf & s & vbcrlf & d
end function

DataSourceModel

public ID as Integer
public Active as Boolean
public ccGuid as String
public ConnString as String

public ContentControlID as Integer
public CreatedBy as Integer
public CreateKey as Integer
public DateAdded as Date



public ModifiedBy as Integer
public ModifiedDate as Date
public Name as String
public SortOrder as String

.ID = cs.getInteger("ID")
.Active = cs.getBoolean("Active")
.ccGuid = cs.getText("ccGuid")
.ConnString = cs.getText("ConnString")

.ContentControlID = cs.getInteger("ContentControlID")
.CreatedBy = cs.getInteger("CreatedBy")
.CreateKey = cs.getInteger("CreateKey")
.DateAdded = cs.getDate("DateAdded")



.ModifiedBy = cs.getInteger("ModifiedBy")
.ModifiedDate = cs.getDate("ModifiedDate")
.Name = cs.getText("Name")
.SortOrder = cs.getText("SortOrder")

cs.setField("Active", Active.ToString())
cs.setField("ccGuid", ccGuid)
cs.setField("ConnString", ConnString)

cs.setField("ContentControlID", ContentControlID.ToString())
cs.setField("CreatedBy", CreatedBy.ToString())
cs.setField("CreateKey", CreateKey.ToString())
cs.setField("DateAdded", DateAdded.ToString())



cs.setField("ModifiedBy", ModifiedBy.ToString())
cs.setField("ModifiedDate", ModifiedDate.ToString())
cs.setField("Name", Name)
cs.setField("SortOrder", SortOrder)
if (String.IsNullOrEmpty(ccGuid)) Then ccGuid = Controllers.genericController.getGUID()

instance.Active = genericController.EncodeBoolean(.fields("Active").defaultValue)
instance.ccGuid = genericController.EncodeText(.fields("ccGuid").defaultValue)
instance.ConnString = genericController.EncodeText(.fields("ConnString").defaultValue)

instance.ContentControlID = cdef.id
instance.CreatedBy = genericController.EncodeInteger(.fields("CreatedBy").defaultValue)
instance.CreateKey = genericController.EncodeInteger(.fields("CreateKey").defaultValue)
instance.DateAdded = genericController.EncodeDate(.fields("DateAdded").defaultValue)



instance.ModifiedBy = genericController.EncodeInteger(.fields("ModifiedBy").defaultValue)
instance.ModifiedDate = genericController.EncodeDate(.fields("ModifiedDate").defaultValue)
instance.Name = genericController.EncodeText(.fields("Name").defaultValue)
instance.SortOrder = genericController.EncodeText(.fields("SortOrder").defaultValue)

ContentFieldHelpModel

public ID as Integer
public Active as Boolean
public ccGuid as String

public ContentControlID as Integer
public CreatedBy as Integer
public CreateKey as Integer
public DateAdded as Date



public FieldID as Integer
public HelpCustom as String
public HelpDefault as String
public ModifiedBy as Integer
public ModifiedDate as Date
public Name as String
